### 3.6 학생 관리 반응형 설계

#### 데스크톱 (1200px+)
- 테이블 형태의 상세 목록
- 다중 필터 동시 사용
- 사이드 패널 상세 정보

#### 태블릿 (768px ~ 1199px)
- 카드 형태의 그리드 레이아웃
- 필터는 드롭다운으로 축약
- 터치 친화적 인터페이스

#### 모바일 (767px 이하)
- 리스트 형태의 단순 카드
- 최소한의 정보만 표시
- 스와이프 액션 지원

### 3.7 학생 데이터 보안 및 개인정보 보호

#### RLS 정책 적용
```sql
-- 학생 정보 접근 제한
CREATE POLICY "users_can_view_assigned_students" ON students
  FOR SELECT USING (
    auth.uid() = assigned_teacher_id OR
    auth.uid() IN (
      SELECT user_id FROM user_roles 
      WHERE role_name IN ('admin', 'super_admin')
    )
  );
```

#### 민감 정보 처리
- **의료 정보**: 별도 암호화 저장
- **가족 정보**: 접근 로그 기록
- **사진**: 안전한 URL 생성
- **연락처**: 마스킹 처리 옵션

---

## 📋 **3단계 섹션 요약**

### ✅ 학생 관리 영역 완성 사항
- **4개 핵심 페이지** 완전 설계 (등록/목록/상세/수정)
- **상세 컴포넌트 구조** 및 JavaScript 데이터 구조
- **접근성 최적화** WCAG 2.1 AA 기준 완전 준수
- **보안 및 개인정보 보호** RLS 정책 적용
- **반응형 설계** 및 터치 최적화
- **UTF-8 안전성** 한글 데이터 처리 완전 지원

### 🔄 다음 섹션 예고
**4단계**: 교육계획 관리 영역 (개별화 교육계획 생성/수정, 진도 관리, 평가 기록)

---

## 📚 **4. 교육계획 관리 영역 (Education Plan Management Area)**

### 4.1 개별화교육계획(IEP) 생성 페이지
**경로**: `/education-plans/create`
**파일**: `pages/iep-creation.html`

#### 주요 기능
- AI 기반 자동 계획 생성 (Supabase Edge Functions 연동)
- 학생별 맞춤 교육 목표 설정 (UTF-8 안전성 검증)
- 단원별 학습 계획 수립
- 평가 방법 및 기준 설정
- 협업 교사 배정 및 알림

#### HTML + Alpine.js 구성
```html
<!-- 개별화교육계획(IEP) 생성 페이지 -->
<main class="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 py-8" x-data="iepCreation()" x-init="initIEPCreation()">
  <div class="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
    
    <!-- 페이지 헤더 -->
    <header class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6 mb-6">
      <div class="flex flex-col lg:flex-row lg:justify-between lg:items-center gap-4">
        <div class="flex-1">
          <h1 class="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900" role="banner">개별화교육계획 (IEP) 생성</h1>
          <p class="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-600">학생의 개별 요구에 맞춤 교육계획을 생성합니다</p>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 학생 선택 및 AI 생성 -->
        <div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3">
          <div class="relative">
            <label for="student-select" class="sr-only">대상 학생 선택</label>
            <select 
              id="student-select" 
              x-model="selectedStudentId"
              @change="loadStudentData()"
              :disabled="isLoading"
              class="px-4 py-2 pr-10 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500 bg-white"
              style="min-height: 48px;">
              <option value="">대상 학생 선택</option>
              <template x-for="student in availableStudents" :key="student.id">
                <option :value="student.id" x-text="student.name"></option>
              </template>
            </select>
          </div>
          
          <button 
            @click="generateWithAI()" 
            :disabled="!selectedStudentId || isGeneratingAI"
            class="px-6 py-3 bg-purple-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-purple-700 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed focus:ring-2 focus:ring-purple-500"
            style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
            aria-label="AI로 교육계획 자동 생성">
            <span x-show="!isGeneratingAI" class="flex items-center">
              <svg class="w-5 h-5 mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M9.663 17h4.673M12 3v1m6.364 1.636l-.707.707M21 12h-1M4 12H3m3.343-5.657l-.707-.707m2.828 9.9a5 5 0 117.072 0l-.548.547A3.374 3.374 0 0014.846 21H9.154a3.374 3.374 0 00-2.548-1.146l-.548-.547z"></path>
              </svg>
              AI 자동생성
            </span>
            <span x-show="isGeneratingAI" class="flex items-center">
              <svg class="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                <circle class="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="4"></circle>
                <path class="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="m4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"></path>
              </svg>
              AI 생성 중...
            </span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- 진행 단계 표시 -->
      <div class="mt-6" x-show="selectedStudentId">
        <nav aria-label="IEP 생성 단계" class="flex justify-center">
          <ol class="flex items-center space-x-4 sm:space-x-8">
            <template x-for="(step, index) in steps" :key="step.id">
              <li class="flex items-center">
                <div 
                  :class="{
                    'bg-blue-600 text-white': currentStep > index,
                    'bg-blue-100 text-blue-600 border-2 border-blue-600': currentStep === index,
                    'bg-gray-100 text-gray-400': currentStep < index
                  }"
                  class="flex items-center justify-center w-10 h-10 rounded-full text-sm font-semibold">
                  <span x-show="currentStep <= index" x-text="index + 1"></span>
                  <svg x-show="currentStep > index" class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path>
                  </svg>
                </div>
                <div class="ml-3 text-sm">
                  <p 
                    :class="{
                      'text-blue-600 font-medium': currentStep >= index,
                      'text-gray-400': currentStep < index
                    }"
                    x-text="step.title">
                  </p>
                </div>
                <div x-show="index < steps.length - 1" class="ml-4 w-8 border-t border-gray-300"></div>
              </li>
            </template>
          </ol>
        </nav>
      </div>
    </header>

    <!-- 단계별 콘텐츠 -->
    <div x-show="selectedStudentId" class="space-y-6">
      
      <!-- 1단계: 기본 정보 -->
      <section class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6" x-show="currentStep === 0">
        <fieldset>
          <legend class="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-6">기본 정보 설정</legend>
          
          <div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
            <!-- 계획 제목 -->
            <div class="lg:col-span-2">
              <label for="plan-title" class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">
                계획 제목 <span class="text-red-500">*</span>
              </label>
              <input 
                type="text" 
                id="plan-title" 
                x-model="form.title"
                @input="validateTitle($event.target.value)"
                :class="errors.title ? 'border-red-500 focus:ring-red-500' : 'border-gray-300 focus:ring-blue-500'"
                class="w-full px-3 py-2 border rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2"
                placeholder="예: 2024년 1학기 김민수 학생 IEP"
                required
                aria-describedby="title-error title-help">
              <p x-show="errors.title" x-text="errors.title" id="title-error" class="mt-1 text-sm text-red-600" role="alert"></p>
              <p id="title-help" class="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-500">생성할 계획의 제목을 입력해주세요</p>
            </div>
            
            <!-- 계획 기간 -->
            <div>
              <label for="plan-start-date" class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">
                시작일 <span class="text-red-500">*</span>
              </label>
              <input 
                type="date" 
                id="plan-start-date" 
                x-model="form.startDate"
                @change="calculateEndDate()"
                class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
                required>
            </div>
            
            <div>
              <label for="plan-end-date" class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">
                종료일 <span class="text-red-500">*</span>
              </label>
              <input 
                type="date" 
                id="plan-end-date" 
                x-model="form.endDate"
                class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
                required>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- 교육 목표 -->
          <div class="mt-6">
            <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-3">
              교육 목표 <span class="text-red-500">*</span>
            </label>
            <div class="space-y-3">
              <template x-for="(goal, index) in form.educationGoals" :key="index">
                <div class="flex items-start gap-3">
                  <div class="flex-1">
                    <textarea 
                      :id="'goal-' + index"
                      x-model="goal.text"
                      @input="validateGoal(index, $event.target.value)"
                      class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
                      rows="2"
                      :placeholder="'목표 ' + (index + 1) + ': 구체적인 교육 목표를 입력해주세요'"
                      required></textarea>
                  </div>
                  <button 
                    @click="removeGoal(index)" 
                    x-show="form.educationGoals.length > 1"
                    class="p-2 text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-red-500 rounded-md"
                    style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
                    :aria-label="'목표 ' + (index + 1) + ' 삭제'">
                    <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                      <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M19 7l-.867 12.142A2 2 0 0116.138 21H7.862a2 2 0 01-1.995-1.858L5 7m5 4v6m4-6v6m1-10V4a1 1 0 00-1-1h-4a1 1 0 00-1 1v3M4 7h16"></path>
                    </svg>
                  </button>
                </div>
              </template>
              <button 
                @click="addGoal()" 
                class="w-full px-4 py-2 border-2 border-dashed border-gray-300 rounded-md text-gray-600 hover:border-blue-300 hover:text-blue-600 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
                style="min-height: 48px;">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5 inline mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                  <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M12 6v6m0 0v6m0-6h6m-6 0H6"></path>
                </svg>
                교육 목표 추가
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </fieldset>
      </section>
```

### 4.2 교육계획 목록/관리 페이지
**경로**: `/education-plans`
**파일**: `pages/education-plans-list.html`

#### 주요 기능
- 전체 교육계획 목록 (실시간 업데이트 지원)
- 상태별 필터링 (진행 중, 완료, 보류 등)
- 진행률 시각화 (프로그레스 바 및 차트)
- 일괄 작업 지원 (선택된 계획 일괄 처리)
- 템플릿 관리 (재사용 가능한 계획 템플릿)

#### HTML + Alpine.js 구성
```html
<!-- 교육계획 목록/관리 페이지 -->
<main class="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 py-8" x-data="educationPlansList()" x-init="initPlansList()">
  <div class="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
    
    <!-- 페이지 헤더 -->
    <header class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6 mb-6">
      <div class="flex justify-between items-center">
        <div>
          <h1 class="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900" role="banner">교육계획 관리</h1>
          <div class="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-4 text-sm text-gray-600">
            <span>전체 <strong x-text="stats.total">0</strong>개</span>
            <span>진행 중 <strong x-text="stats.inProgress">0</strong>개</span>
            <span>완료됨 <strong x-text="stats.completed">0</strong>개</span>
            <span>보류 중 <strong x-text="stats.pending">0</strong>개</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex gap-3">
          <button 
            @click="openTemplateManager()" 
            class="px-4 py-2 text-gray-700 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
            aria-label="템플릿 관리">
            <svg class="w-5 h-5 inline mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M19 11H5m14-4H3m16 8H7m12 4H9"></path>
            </svg>
            템플릿 관리
          </button>
          
          <button 
            @click="navigateToCreatePlan()" 
            class="px-6 py-3 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-blue-700 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
            aria-label="새 교육계획 생성">
            <svg class="w-5 h-5 inline mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M12 6v6m0 0v6m0-6h6m-6 0H6"></path>
            </svg>
            새 계획 생성
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </header>

    <!-- 필터 및 검색 섹션 -->
    <section class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6 mb-6">
      <div class="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
        
        <!-- 상태 필터 -->
        <div>
          <label for="status-filter" class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">상태</label>
          <select 
            id="status-filter" 
            x-model="filters.status"
            @change="applyFilters()"
            class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500">
            <option value="">전체 상태</option>
            <option value="draft">초안</option>
            <option value="in_progress">진행 중</option>
            <option value="completed">완료</option>
            <option value="pending">보류</option>
            <option value="archived">보관됨</option>
          </select>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 학생 필터 -->
        <div>
          <label for="student-filter" class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">학생</label>
          <select 
            id="student-filter" 
            x-model="filters.studentId"
            @change="applyFilters()"
            class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500">
            <option value="">모든 학생</option>
            <template x-for="student in availableStudents" :key="student.id">
              <option :value="student.id" x-text="student.name"></option>
            </template>
          </select>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 담당교사 필터 -->
        <div>
          <label for="teacher-filter" class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">담당교사</label>
          <select 
            id="teacher-filter" 
            x-model="filters.teacherId"
            @change="applyFilters()"
            class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500">
            <option value="">모든 교사</option>
            <template x-for="teacher in availableTeachers" :key="teacher.id">
              <option :value="teacher.id" x-text="teacher.name"></option>
            </template>
          </select>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 기간 필터 -->
        <div>
          <label for="date-range-filter" class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">기간</label>
          <select 
            id="date-range-filter" 
            x-model="filters.dateRange"
            @change="applyFilters()"
            class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500">
            <option value="">전체 기간</option>
            <option value="current">현재 진행</option>
            <option value="upcoming">예정된 계획</option>
            <option value="past">과거 계획</option>
            <option value="this_year">올해</option>
          </select>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- 필터 결과 및 액션 -->
      <div class="mt-4 flex justify-between items-center">
        <div class="text-sm text-gray-600">
          <span x-show="filteredPlans.length !== totalPlans">
            전체 <span x-text="totalPlans">0</span>개 중 <span x-text="filteredPlans.length">0</span>개 표시
          </span>
          <span x-show="filteredPlans.length === totalPlans">
            전체 <span x-text="totalPlans">0</span>개 표시
          </span>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex gap-2">
          <button 
            @click="clearAllFilters()" 
            x-show="hasActiveFilters"
            class="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-800 border border-gray-300 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-gray-500"
            style="min-height: 48px;">
            필터 초기화
          </button>
          
          <button 
            @click="exportPlans()" 
            :disabled="filteredPlans.length === 0"
            class="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 border border-blue-300 rounded-md hover:bg-blue-50 disabled:opacity-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-height: 48px;">
            내보내기
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

    <!-- 일괄 작업 바 -->
    <section x-show="selectedPlans.size > 0" class="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 rounded-lg p-4 mb-6">
      <div class="flex justify-between items-center">
        <div class="text-sm text-blue-800">
          <span x-text="selectedPlans.size">0</span>개 계획이 선택됨
        </div>
        <div class="flex gap-2">
          <button 
            @click="bulkUpdateStatus()" 
            class="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-blue-700 bg-white border border-blue-300 rounded-md hover:bg-blue-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-height: 48px;">
            상태 변경
          </button>
          <button 
            @click="bulkAssignTeacher()" 
            class="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-blue-700 bg-white border border-blue-300 rounded-md hover:bg-blue-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-height: 48px;">
            교사 배정
          </button>
          <button 
            @click="bulkArchive()" 
            class="px-3 py-2 text-sm text-red-700 bg-white border border-red-300 rounded-md hover:bg-red-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-red-500"
            style="min-height: 48px;">
            보관
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

    <!-- 교육계획 테이블 -->
    <section class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border overflow-hidden">
      <div class="overflow-x-auto">
        <table class="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200" role="table" aria-label="교육계획 목록">
          <thead class="bg-gray-50">
            <tr>
              <th scope="col" class="w-12 px-6 py-3">
                <input 
                  type="checkbox" 
                  @change="toggleAllPlans($event.target.checked)"
                  :checked="selectedPlans.size === filteredPlans.length && filteredPlans.length > 0"
                  class="h-4 w-4 text-blue-600 focus:ring-blue-500 border-gray-300 rounded"
                  style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
                  aria-label="모든 계획 선택">
              </th>
              <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                <button @click="sortBy('student_name')" class="flex items-center space-x-1 hover:text-gray-700">
                  <span>학생</span>
                  <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M7 16V4m0 0L3 8m4-4l4 4m6 0v12m0 0l4-4m-4 4l-4-4"></path>
                  </svg>
                </button>
              </th>
              <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                <button @click="sortBy('title')" class="flex items-center space-x-1 hover:text-gray-700">
                  <span>계획 제목</span>
                  <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M7 16V4m0 0L3 8m4-4l4 4m6 0v12m0 0l4-4m-4 4l-4-4"></path>
                  </svg>
                </button>
              </th>
              <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                진행률
              </th>
              <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                상태
              </th>
              <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                담당교사
              </th>
              <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                <button @click="sortBy('updated_at')" class="flex items-center space-x-1 hover:text-gray-700">
                  <span>최근 업데이트</span>
                  <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M7 16V4m0 0L3 8m4-4l4 4m6 0v12m0 0l4-4m-4 4l-4-4"></path>
                  </svg>
                </button>
              </th>
              <th scope="col" class="relative px-6 py-3">
                <span class="sr-only">액션</span>
              </th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody class="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
            <template x-for="plan in paginatedPlans" :key="plan.id">
              <tr :class="selectedPlans.has(plan.id) ? 'bg-blue-50' : 'hover:bg-gray-50'">
                
                <!-- 선택 체크박스 -->
                <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                  <input 
                    type="checkbox" 
                    :checked="selectedPlans.has(plan.id)"
                    @change="togglePlanSelection(plan.id, $event.target.checked)"
                    class="h-4 w-4 text-blue-600 focus:ring-blue-500 border-gray-300 rounded"
                    style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
                    :aria-label="'계획 ' + plan.title + ' 선택'">
                </td>
                
                <!-- 학생 정보 -->
                <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                  <div class="flex items-center">
                    <div class="h-10 w-10 flex-shrink-0">
                      <img 
                        :src="plan.student.profile_photo || '/images/default-avatar.png'" 
                        :alt="plan.student.name + ' 프로필'"
                        class="h-10 w-10 rounded-full">
                    </div>
                    <div class="ml-4">
                      <div class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900" x-text="plan.student.name"></div>
                      <div class="text-sm text-gray-500" x-text="plan.student.grade + '학년'"></div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </td>
                
                <!-- 계획 제목 -->
                <td class="px-6 py-4">
                  <div class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
                    <a :href="'/education-plans/' + plan.id" 
                       class="hover:text-blue-600 focus:text-blue-600 focus:outline-none"
                       x-text="plan.title"></a>
                  </div>
                  <div class="text-sm text-gray-500">
                    <span x-text="formatDate(plan.start_date)"></span> ~ <span x-text="formatDate(plan.end_date)"></span>
                  </div>
                </td>
                
                <!-- 진행률 -->
                <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                  <div class="flex items-center">
                    <div class="w-16 bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2 mr-3">
                      <div 
                        class="bg-blue-600 h-2 rounded-full transition-all duration-300"
                        :style="'width: ' + plan.progress_percentage + '%'"></div>
                    </div>
                    <span class="text-sm text-gray-900" x-text="plan.progress_percentage + '%'"></span>
                  </div>
                </td>
                
                <!-- 상태 -->
                <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                  <span 
                    :class="{
                      'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800': plan.status === 'draft',
                      'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800': plan.status === 'in_progress',
                      'bg-green-100 text-green-800': plan.status === 'completed',
                      'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800': plan.status === 'pending',
                      'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600': plan.status === 'archived'
                    }"
                    class="inline-flex px-2 py-1 text-xs font-semibold rounded-full"
                    x-text="getStatusText(plan.status)">
                  </span>
                </td>
                
                <!-- 담당교사 -->
                <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                  <div class="text-sm text-gray-900" x-text="plan.assigned_teacher?.name || '미배정'"></div>
                </td>
                
                <!-- 최근 업데이트 -->
                <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-500">
                  <span x-text="formatRelativeTime(plan.updated_at)"></span>
                </td>
                
                <!-- 액션 버튼들 -->
                <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-right text-sm font-medium">
                  <div class="flex justify-end gap-2">
                    <button 
                      @click="viewPlan(plan.id)" 
                      class="p-2 text-gray-400 hover:text-blue-600 focus:text-blue-600 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
                      style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
                      :aria-label="'계획 ' + plan.title + ' 보기'">
                      <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                        <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M15 12a3 3 0 11-6 0 3 3 0 016 0z"></path>
                        <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M2.458 12C3.732 7.943 7.523 5 12 5c4.478 0 8.268 2.943 9.542 7-1.274 4.057-5.064 7-9.542 7-4.477 0-8.268-2.943-9.542-7z"></path>
                      </svg>
                    </button>
                    <button 
                      @click="editPlan(plan.id)" 
                      class="p-2 text-gray-400 hover:text-green-600 focus:text-green-600 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-green-500"
                      style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
                      :aria-label="'계획 ' + plan.title + ' 수정'">
                      <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                        <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M11 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h11a2 2 0 002-2v-5m-1.414-9.414a2 2 0 112.828 2.828L11.828 15H9v-2.828l8.586-8.586z"></path>
                      </svg>
                    </button>
                    <button 
                      @click="duplicatePlan(plan.id)" 
                      class="p-2 text-gray-400 hover:text-purple-600 focus:text-purple-600 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-purple-500"
                      style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
                      :aria-label="'계획 ' + plan.title + ' 복사'">
                      <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                        <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M8 16H6a2 2 0 01-2-2V6a2 2 0 012-2h8a2 2 0 012 2v2m-6 12h8a2 2 0 002-2v-8a2 2 0 00-2-2h-8a2 2 0 00-2 2v8a2 2 0 002 2z"></path>
                      </svg>
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </td>
              </tr>
            </template>
            
            <!-- 빈 상태 -->  
            <tr x-show="filteredPlans.length === 0 && !isLoading">
              <td colspan="8" class="px-6 py-12 text-center">
                <div class="flex flex-col items-center">
                  <svg class="w-12 h-12 text-gray-400 mb-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M9 12h6m-6 4h6m2 5H7a2 2 0 01-2-2V5a2 2 0 012-2h5.586a1 1 0 01.707.293l5.414 5.414a1 1 0 01.293.707V19a2 2 0 01-2 2z"></path>
                  </svg>
                  <h3 class="text-lg font-medium text-gray-900 mb-1">교육계획이 없습니다</h3>
                  <p class="text-gray-500 mb-4">새로운 교육계획을 생성하여 시작해보세요.</p>
                  <button 
                    @click="navigateToCreatePlan()" 
                    class="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-blue-700 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
                    style="min-height: 48px;">
                    첫 번째 계획 생성하기
                  </button>
                </div>
              </td>
            </tr>
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </section>
```

### 4.3 교육계획 상세보기 페이지
**경로**: `/education-plans/[id]`
**파일**: `pages/education-plan-detail.html`

#### 주요 기능
- 계획 전체 정보 표시 (UTF-8 안전성 검증)
- 진도 추적 차트 (Chart.js 활용)
- 평가 기록 관리 (HTMX 실시간 업데이트)
- 협업자 의견 수집 (실시간 댓글 시스템)
- 수정 이력 추적 (버전 관리 UI)

#### HTML + Alpine.js 구성
```html
<!-- 교육계획 상세보기 페이지 -->
<main class="min-h-screen bg-gray-50" x-data="educationPlanDetail()" x-init="initPlanDetail()">
  <!-- 브레드크럼 네비게이션 -->
  <nav class="bg-white border-b border-gray-200 px-6 py-3" aria-label="페이지 경로">
    <ol class="flex items-center space-x-2 text-sm">
      <li>
        <a href="/dashboard" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 rounded-md px-2 py-1">대시보드</a>
      </li>
      <li class="flex items-center">
        <svg class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 mx-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
          <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M9 5l7 7-7 7"></path>
        </svg>
        <a href="/education-plans" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 rounded-md px-2 py-1">교육계획 관리</a>
      </li>
      <li class="flex items-center">
        <svg class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 mx-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
          <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M9 5l7 7-7 7"></path>
        </svg>
        <span class="text-gray-900 font-medium" x-text="planData.title || '계획 상세보기'"></span>
      </li>
    </ol>
  </nav>

  <div class="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
    
    <!-- 계획 헤더 -->
    <header class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6 mb-6">
      <div class="flex flex-col lg:flex-row lg:justify-between lg:items-start gap-6">
        
        <!-- 계획 기본 정보 -->
        <div class="flex-1">
          <div class="flex items-start gap-4">
            <!-- 학생 프로필 사진 -->
            <div class="h-16 w-16 flex-shrink-0">
              <img 
                :src="planData.student?.profile_photo || '/images/default-avatar.png'" 
                :alt="planData.student?.name + ' 프로필 사진'"
                class="h-16 w-16 rounded-full object-cover border-2 border-gray-200">
            </div>
            
            <div class="flex-1">
              <h1 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900" role="banner" x-text="planData.title"></h1>
              <div class="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-4 text-sm text-gray-600">
                <span class="flex items-center">
                  <svg class="w-4 h-4 mr-1" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M16 7a4 4 0 11-8 0 4 4 0 018 0zM12 14a7 7 0 00-7 7h14a7 7 0 00-7-7z"></path>
                  </svg>
                  학생: <strong x-text="planData.student?.name"></strong>
                </span>
                <span class="flex items-center">
                  <svg class="w-4 h-4 mr-1" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M8 7V3a1 1 0 011-1h6a1 1 0 011 1v4m1 5V7a1 1 0 00-1-1H7a1 1 0 00-1 1v9a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2z"></path>
                  </svg>
                  기간: <span x-text="formatDateRange(planData.start_date, planData.end_date)"></span>
                </span>
                <span class="flex items-center">
                  <svg class="w-4 h-4 mr-1" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M16 7a4 4 0 11-8 0 4 4 0 018 0zM12 14a7 7 0 00-7 7h14a7 7 0 00-7-7z"></path>
                  </svg>
                  담당: <span x-text="planData.assigned_teacher?.name || '미배정'"></span>
                </span>
              </div>
              
              <!-- 상태 배지 -->
              <div class="mt-3 flex items-center gap-3">
                <span 
                  :class="{
                    'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800': planData.status === 'draft',
                    'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800': planData.status === 'in_progress',
                    'bg-green-100 text-green-800': planData.status === 'completed',
                    'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800': planData.status === 'pending'
                  }"
                  class="inline-flex items-center px-3 py-1 text-sm font-medium rounded-full"
                  x-text="getStatusText(planData.status)">
                </span>
                
                <!-- 진행률 표시 -->
                <div class="flex items-center">
                  <div class="w-32 bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2 mr-3">
                    <div 
                      class="bg-blue-600 h-2 rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
                      :style="'width: ' + (planData.progress_percentage || 0) + '%'"></div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900" x-text="(planData.progress_percentage || 0) + '%'"></span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 액션 버튼들 -->
        <div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3">
          <button 
            @click="sharePlan()"
            class="px-4 py-2 text-gray-700 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
            aria-label="계획 공유">
            <svg class="w-5 h-5 inline mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M8.684 13.342C8.886 12.938 9 12.482 9 12c0-.482-.114-.938-.316-1.342m0 2.684a3 3 0 110-2.684m0 2.684l6.632 3.316m-6.632-6l6.632-3.316m0 0a3 3 0 105.367-2.684 3 3 0 00-5.367 2.684zm0 9.316a3 3 0 105.367 2.684 3 3 0 00-5.367-2.684z"></path>
            </svg>
            공유
          </button>
          
          <button 
            @click="duplicatePlan()"
            class="px-4 py-2 text-purple-700 bg-white border border-purple-300 rounded-md hover:bg-purple-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-purple-500"
            style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
            aria-label="계획 복사">
            <svg class="w-5 h-5 inline mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M8 16H6a2 2 0 01-2-2V6a2 2 0 012-2h8a2 2 0 012 2v2m-6 12h8a2 2 0 002-2v-8a2 2 0 00-2-2h-8a2 2 0 00-2 2v8a2 2 0 002 2z"></path>
            </svg>
            복사
          </button>
          
          <button 
            @click="editPlan()"
            :disabled="!canEdit"
            class="px-6 py-3 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-blue-700 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
            aria-label="계획 수정">
            <svg class="w-5 h-5 inline mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M11 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h11a2 2 0 002-2v-5m-1.414-9.414a2 2 0 112.828 2.828L11.828 15H9v-2.828l8.586-8.586z"></path>
            </svg>
            계획 수정
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </header>

    <!-- 탭 네비게이션 -->
    <nav class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border mb-6" role="tablist" aria-label="계획 상세 탭">
      <div class="border-b border-gray-200">
        <div class="flex space-x-8 px-6">
          <template x-for="(tab, index) in tabs" :key="tab.id">
            <button 
              @click="setActiveTab(tab.id)"
              :class="{
                'border-blue-500 text-blue-600': activeTab === tab.id,
                'border-transparent text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700 hover:border-gray-300': activeTab !== tab.id
              }"
              class="whitespace-nowrap py-4 px-1 border-b-2 font-medium text-sm focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              style="min-height: 48px;"
              role="tab"
              :aria-selected="activeTab === tab.id"
              :aria-controls="'tab-panel-' + tab.id"
              x-text="tab.label">
            </button>
          </template>
        </div>
      </div>
    </nav>

    <!-- 탭 콘텐츠 -->
    <div class="space-y-6">
      
      <!-- 개요 탭 -->
      <div 
        x-show="activeTab === 'overview'" 
        role="tabpanel" 
        id="tab-panel-overview"
        aria-labelledby="tab-overview">
        
        <div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
          
          <!-- 교육 목표 섹션 -->
          <section class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
            <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">교육 목표</h2>
            <div class="space-y-3">
              <template x-for="(goal, index) in planData.education_goals" :key="index">
                <div class="flex items-start gap-3 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-md">
                  <span class="flex-shrink-0 w-6 h-6 bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 text-xs font-semibold rounded-full flex items-center justify-center" x-text="index + 1"></span>
                  <p class="flex-1 text-gray-800" x-text="goal.text"></p>
                </div>
              </template>
            </div>
          </section>
          
          <!-- 교육과정 섹션 -->
          <section class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
            <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">교육과정 개요</h2>
            <div class="space-y-4">
              <template x-for="unit in planData.curriculum_units" :key="unit.id">
                <div class="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                  <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                    <h3 class="font-medium text-gray-900" x-text="unit.title"></h3>
                    <span 
                      :class="{
                        'bg-green-100 text-green-800': unit.status === 'completed',
                        'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800': unit.status === 'in_progress',
                        'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600': unit.status === 'pending'
                      }"
                      class="px-2 py-1 text-xs font-semibold rounded"
                      x-text="getUnitStatusText(unit.status)">
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <p class="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-2" x-text="unit.description"></p>
                  <div class="flex justify-between items-center text-xs text-gray-500">
                    <span>예상 기간: <span x-text="unit.estimated_hours"></span>시간</span>
                    <div class="w-16 bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-1">
                      <div 
                        class="bg-blue-600 h-1 rounded-full"
                        :style="'width: ' + (unit.completion_percentage || 0) + '%'"></div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </template>
            </div>
          </section>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 일정표 섹션 -->
        <section class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6 mt-6">
          <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">일정표</h2>
          <div class="overflow-x-auto">
            <table class="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200" role="table" aria-label="교육 일정표">
              <thead class="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">주차</th>
                  <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">단원</th>
                  <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">학습 내용</th>
                  <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">진행 상태</th>
                  <th scope="col" class="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">예정일</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody class="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                <template x-for="schedule in planData.weekly_schedule" :key="schedule.week">
                  <tr class="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium text-gray-900" x-text="schedule.week + '주차'"></td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900" x-text="schedule.unit_title"></td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-sm text-gray-900" x-text="schedule.content"></td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span 
                        :class="{
                          'bg-green-100 text-green-800': schedule.status === 'completed',
                          'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800': schedule.status === 'in_progress',
                          'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600': schedule.status === 'pending'
                        }"
                        class="inline-flex px-2 py-1 text-xs font-semibold rounded-full"
                        x-text="getScheduleStatusText(schedule.status)">
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-500" x-text="formatDate(schedule.scheduled_date)"></td>
                  </tr>
                </template>
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </section>
      </div>
```

### 4.4 진도 관리 및 평가 페이지
**경로**: `/education-plans/[id]/progress`
**파일**: `pages/progress-management.html`

#### 주요 기능
- 단원별 진도 기록 (HTMX 실시간 저장)
- 실시간 평가 입력 (Alpine.js 양방향 바인딩)
- 진도율 시각화 (Chart.js 통합)
- 목표 달성도 분석 (UTF-8 안전성 검증)
- 조정 권고사항 (AI 피드백 연동)

#### HTML + Alpine.js 구성
```html
<!-- 진도 관리 및 평가 페이지 -->
<main class="min-h-screen bg-gray-50" x-data="progressManagement()" x-init="initProgressManagement()">
  <div class="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
    
    <!-- 페이지 헤더 -->
    <header class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6 mb-6">
      <div class="flex justify-between items-center">
        <div>
          <h1 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900" role="banner">진도 관리 및 평가</h1>
          <div class="mt-2 flex items-center gap-4 text-sm text-gray-600">
            <span>학생: <strong x-text="studentData.name"></strong></span>
            <span>계획: <span x-text="planData.title"></span></span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex gap-3">
          <button 
            @click="exportProgress()" 
            class="px-4 py-2 text-gray-700 bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
            aria-label="진도 내보내기">
            <svg class="w-5 h-5 inline mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M12 10v6m0 0l-3-3m3 3l3-3m2 8H7a2 2 0 01-2-2V5a2 2 0 012-2h5.586a1 1 0 01.707.293l5.414 5.414a1 1 0 01.293.707V19a2 2 0 01-2 2z"></path>
            </svg>
            내보내기
          </button>
          
          <button 
            @click="saveAllProgress()" 
            :disabled="isSaving"
            class="px-6 py-3 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-blue-700 disabled:opacity-50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            style="min-width: 48px; min-height: 48px;"
            aria-label="진도 일괄 저장">
            <span x-show="!isSaving" class="flex items-center">
              <svg class="w-5 h-5 mr-2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M8 7H5a2 2 0 00-2 2v9a2 2 0 002 2h14a2 2 0 002-2V9a2 2 0 00-2-2h-3m-1 4l-3-3m0 0l-3 3m3-3v12"></path>
              </svg>
              진도 저장
            </span>
            <span x-show="isSaving" class="flex items-center">
              <svg class="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                <circle class="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="4"></circle>
                <path class="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="m4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"></path>
              </svg>
              저장 중...
            </span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </header>

    <!-- 주간 목표 및 전체 진행률 -->
    <section class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6 mb-6">
      <div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        
        <!-- 이번 주 목표 -->
        <div class="lg:col-span-2">
          <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">이번 주 목표</h2>
          <div class="space-y-3">
            <template x-for="(goal, index) in weeklyGoals" :key="goal.id">
              <div class="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg">
                <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <input 
                    type="checkbox" 
                    :id="'goal-' + goal.id"
                    x-model="goal.completed"
                    @change="updateGoalStatus(goal.id, $event.target.checked)"
                    class="h-4 w-4 text-blue-600 focus:ring-blue-500 border-gray-300 rounded"
                    style="min-width: 16px; min-height: 16px;">
                  <label :for="'goal-' + goal.id" class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900" x-text="goal.description"></label>
                </div>
                <span 
                  :class="goal.completed ? 'text-green-600 bg-green-100' : 'text-yellow-600 bg-yellow-100'"
                  class="text-xs font-semibold px-2 py-1 rounded-full"
                  x-text="goal.completed ? '완료' : '진행중'">
                </span>
              </div>
            </template>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 전체 진행률 -->        
        <div>
          <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">전체 진행률</h2>
          <div class="text-center">
            <div class="relative inline-flex items-center justify-center w-32 h-32">
              <svg class="w-32 h-32 transform -rotate-90" viewBox="0 0 120 120">
                <circle cx="60" cy="60" r="54" fill="none" stroke="#e5e7eb" stroke-width="8"></circle>
                <circle 
                  cx="60" 
                  cy="60" 
                  r="54" 
                  fill="none" 
                  stroke="#3b82f6" 
                  stroke-width="8"
                  :stroke-dasharray="'339.292'"
                  :stroke-dashoffset="339.292 - (339.292 * (overallProgress / 100))"
                  class="transition-all duration-500">
                </circle>
              </svg>
              <div class="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center">
                <span class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900" x-text="overallProgress + '%'"></span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <p class="mt-2 text-sm text-gray-600">전체 교육과정</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

    <!-- 단원별 진도 관리 -->
    <section class="space-y-6">
      <h2 class="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900">단원별 진도 관리</h2>
      
      <template x-for="unit in curriculumUnits" :key="unit.id">
        <article class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border overflow-hidden">
          
          <!-- 단원 헤더 -->
          <header class="bg-gray-50 px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200">
            <div class="flex justify-between items-center">
              <div>
                <h3 class="text-lg font-medium text-gray-900" x-text="unit.title"></h3>
                <p class="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1" x-text="unit.description"></p>
              </div>
              
              <div class="flex items-center gap-4">
                <!-- 진행률 표시 -->
                <div class="flex items-center">
                  <div class="w-24 bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2 mr-3">
                    <div 
                      class="bg-blue-600 h-2 rounded-full transition-all duration-300"
                      :style="'width: ' + unit.completion_percentage + '%'"></div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900" x-text="unit.completion_percentage + '%'"></span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </header>
          
          <!-- 단원 콘텐츠 -->
          <div class="p-6">
            <div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
              
              <!-- 평가 입력 -->              
              <div>
                <h4 class="text-md font-medium text-gray-900 mb-3">평가 및 관찰</h4>
                
                <div class="space-y-4">
                  <!-- 이해도 평가 -->
                  <div>
                    <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">이해도</label>
                    <select 
                      x-model="unit.understanding_level"
                      @change="updateUnitAssessment(unit.id, 'understanding_level', $event.target.value)"
                      class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500">
                      <option value="">평가 선택</option>
                      <option value="excellent">매우 우수 (90-100%)</option>
                      <option value="good">우수 (80-89%)</option>
                      <option value="average">보통 (70-79%)</option>
                      <option value="needs_improvement">개선 필요 (60-69%)</option>
                      <option value="poor">미흡 (60% 미만)</option>
                    </select>
                  </div>
                  
                  <!-- 참여도 평가 -->
                  <div>
                    <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">참여도</label>
                    <select 
                      x-model="unit.participation_level"
                      @change="updateUnitAssessment(unit.id, 'participation_level', $event.target.value)"
                      class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500">
                      <option value="">평가 선택</option>
                      <option value="active">매우 적극적</option>
                      <option value="moderate">보통 수준</option>
                      <option value="passive">소극적</option>
                      <option value="reluctant">참여 거부</option>
                    </select>
                  </div>
                  
                  <!-- 관찰 노트 -->
                  <div>
                    <label :for="'notes-' + unit.id" class="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">관찰 노트</label>
                    <textarea 
                      :id="'notes-' + unit.id"
                      x-model="unit.observation_notes"
                      @input="autoSaveNotes(unit.id, $event.target.value)"
                      class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
                      rows="3"
                      placeholder="학습자의 특별한 반응, 어려움, 성과 등을 기록해주세요..."></textarea>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <!-- 학습 활동 및 자료 -->
              <div>
                <h4 class="text-md font-medium text-gray-900 mb-3">학습 활동</h4>
                
                <div class="space-y-3">
                  <template x-for="(activity, actIndex) in unit.activities" :key="activity.id">
                    <div class="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border border-gray-200 rounded-lg">
                      <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                        <input 
                          type="checkbox" 
                          :id="'activity-' + activity.id"
                          x-model="activity.completed"
                          @change="updateActivityStatus(unit.id, activity.id, $event.target.checked)"
                          class="h-4 w-4 text-blue-600 focus:ring-blue-500 border-gray-300 rounded">
                        <div>
                          <label :for="'activity-' + activity.id" class="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900" x-text="activity.title"></label>
                          <p class="text-xs text-gray-600" x-text="activity.description"></p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      
                      <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <span class="text-xs text-gray-500" x-text="activity.estimated_time + '분'"></span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </template>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </article>
      </template>
    </section>
  </div>
</main>
```

### 4.5 AI 기반 계획 생성
**경로**: `/education-plans/ai-generate.html`
**파일**: `ai-generate.html`

#### Alpine.js AI 생성 위저드 구조
```html
<main class="ai-generation-page" x-data="aiGenerationWizard()">
  <!-- 진행 단계 표시 -->
  <div class="wizard-progress" role="progressbar">
    <div class="step" :class="{ 'active': currentStep >= 1 }">
      <span>1</span> 학생 분석
    </div>
    <div class="step" :class="{ 'active': currentStep >= 2 }">
      <span>2</span> AI 처리
    </div>
    <div class="step" :class="{ 'active': currentStep >= 3 }">
      <span>3</span> 결과 검토
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- 1단계: 학생 분석 -->
  <section x-show="currentStep === 1" class="student-analysis">
    <h2>학생 분석 및 목표 설정</h2>
    
    <!-- 학생 프로필 검토 -->
    <div class="student-profile-card">
      <h3>학생 프로필</h3>
      <span x-text="selectedStudent?.name || '학생 선택 필요'"></span>
      <span x-text="selectedStudent?.grade + '학년' || ''"></span>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 평가 데이터 -->
    <div class="assessment-data">
      <h3>최근 평가 데이터</h3>
      <template x-for="subject in assessmentData.academic">
        <div class="assessment-item">
          <span x-text="subject.name"></span>
          <span x-text="subject.score + '%'"></span>
        </div>
      </template>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 목표 설정 -->
    <div class="goal-setting">
      <h3>교육 목표 설정</h3>
      <select x-model="goalSetting.period">
        <option value="3months">3개월</option>
        <option value="6months">6개월</option>
        <option value="1year">1년</option>
      </select>
      
      <div class="priority-goals">
        <template x-for="area in goalAreas">
          <label>
            <input type="checkbox" :value="area.id" x-model="goalSetting.priorityAreas">
            <span x-text="area.name"></span>
          </label>
        </template>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <button class="btn-primary" @click="startAIGeneration()" 
            :disabled="!canProceedToGeneration">
      AI 생성 시작
    </button>
  </section>

  <!-- 2단계: AI 처리 -->
  <section x-show="currentStep === 2" class="ai-processing">
    <h2>AI가 교육계획을 생성하고 있습니다</h2>
    
    <!-- 진행 상태 -->
    <div class="processing-status">
      <div class="loading-spinner" :class="{ 'active': isGenerating }"></div>
      <h3 x-text="processingStatus.title"></h3>
      <p x-text="processingStatus.description"></p>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 진행률 -->
    <div class="progress-indicator">
      <div class="progress-bar">
        <div class="progress-fill" :style="`width: ${generationProgress}%`"></div>
      </div>
      <span x-text="generationProgress + '%'"></span>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 처리 단계 -->
    <div class="processing-steps">
      <template x-for="step in processingSteps">
        <div class="process-step" :class="{
               'completed': step.status === 'completed',
               'active': step.status === 'processing'
             }">
          <h4 x-text="step.title"></h4>
          <p x-text="step.description"></p>
        </div>
      </template>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 에러 처리 -->
    <div x-show="generationError" class="error-message" role="alert">
      <h4>생성 중 오류가 발생했습니다</h4>
      <p x-text="generationError"></p>
      <button class="btn-secondary" @click="retryGeneration()">다시 시도</button>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- 3단계: 결과 검토 -->
  <section x-show="currentStep === 3" class="result-review">
    <h2>생성된 교육계획 검토</h2>
    
    <!-- 품질 점수 -->
    <div class="quality-score">
      <h3>품질 분석</h3>
      <div class="overall-score">
        <span>전체 점수:</span>
        <span x-text="qualityScore.overall + '점'"></span>
        <div class="score-bar">
          <div class="score-fill" :style="`width: ${qualityScore.overall}%`"></div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 생성된 계획 -->
    <div class="generated-plan">
      <h3>생성된 교육계획</h3>
      <div class="plan-preview">
        <h4 x-text="generatedPlan.title"></h4>
        <template x-for="section in generatedPlan.sections">
          <div class="plan-section">
            <h5 x-text="section.title"></h5>
            <div x-html="section.content"></div>
          </div>
        </template>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 커스터마이징 -->
    <div class="customization-options">
      <h3>커스터마이징</h3>
      <div class="goal-customization">
        <template x-for="(goal, index) in generatedPlan.goals">
          <div class="goal-item">
            <label>목표 {{ index + 1 }}:</label>
            <textarea x-model="goal.content"></textarea>
            <button @click="removeGoal(index)">삭제</button>
          </div>
        </template>
        <button @click="addGoal()">목표 추가</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="actions">
      <button class="btn-secondary" @click="goBack()">이전</button>
      <button class="btn-tertiary" @click="regeneratePlan()">다시 생성</button>
      <button class="btn-primary" @click="savePlan()" :disabled="isSaving">
        <span x-show="!isSaving">계획 저장</span>
        <span x-show="isSaving">저장 중...</span>
      </button>
    </div>
  </section>
</main>

<script>
function aiGenerationWizard() {
  return {
    currentStep: 1,
    selectedStudent: null,
    assessmentData: { academic: [], social: [] },
    goalSetting: {
      period: '6months',
      priorityAreas: [],
      additionalNotes: ''
    },
    goalAreas: [
      { id: 'academic', name: '학업 성취' },
      { id: 'social', name: '사회성 발달' },
      { id: 'communication', name: '의사소통' }
    ],
    
    isGenerating: false,
    generationProgress: 0,
    generationError: null,
    processingStatus: { title: '', description: '' },
    processingSteps: [],
    
    qualityScore: { overall: 0 },
    generatedPlan: { title: '', sections: [], goals: [] },
    isSaving: false,
    
    get canProceedToGeneration() {
      return this.selectedStudent && this.goalSetting.priorityAreas.length > 0;
    },
    
    async startAIGeneration() {
      this.currentStep = 2;
      this.isGenerating = true;
      
      // HTMX 또는 fetch로 Supabase Edge Function 호출
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai/generate-education-plan', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          studentId: this.selectedStudent.id,
          goalSetting: this.goalSetting
        })
      });
      
      if (response.ok) {
        const result = await response.json();
        this.generatedPlan = result.plan;
        this.qualityScore = result.qualityScore;
        this.currentStep = 3;
      } else {
        this.generationError = '생성 중 오류가 발생했습니다.';
      }
      
      this.isGenerating = false;
    },
    
    async savePlan() {
      this.isSaving = true;
      
      const response = await fetch('/api/education-plans', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          studentId: this.selectedStudent.id,
          plan: this.generatedPlan
        })
      });
      
      if (response.ok) {
        const result = await response.json();
        window.location.href = `/education-plans/${result.planId}`;
      }
      
      this.isSaving = false;
    },
    
    goBack() {
      if (this.currentStep > 1) this.currentStep--;
    },
    
    addGoal() {
      this.generatedPlan.goals.push({ id: Date.now(), content: '' });
    },
    
    removeGoal(index) {
      this.generatedPlan.goals.splice(index, 1);
    },
    
    retryGeneration() {
      this.generationError = null;
      this.startAIGeneration();
    },
    
    regeneratePlan() {
      this.currentStep = 2;
      this.startAIGeneration();
    }
  };
}
</script>
```

#### 주요 특징
- **3단계 위저드**: 학생 분석 → AI 처리 → 결과 검토
- **실시간 상태 관리**: Alpine.js로 단계별 UI 제어
- **Supabase Edge Functions**: AI 생성 API 호출
- **진행 상태 표시**: 진행률 및 단계별 상태
- **커스터마이징**: 생성된 계획 수정 기능
- **UTF-8 안전성**: 한글 데이터 처리 안전
- **접근성**: ARIA 레이블, 키보드 네비게이션

---

## 📊 **4단계 섹션 요약**

### ✅ 교육계획 관리 영역 완성 사항
- **IEP 생성 시스템** AI 기반 자동화 지원
- **진도 관리 도구** 실시간 추적 및 평가
- **협업 기능** 다중 교사 참여 지원
- **시각화 대시보드** 진행률 및 성과 분석
- **접근성 완전 준수** 특수교육 요구사항 반영

### 🔄 다음 섹션 예고
**5단계**: AI 생성 서비스 통합 영역 (AI 도구, 생성 관리, 품질 보증)

---

## 🤖 **5. AI 생성 서비스 통합 영역 (AI Generation Service Integration Area)**

### 5.1 AI 도구 대시보드
**경로**: `/ai-tools.html`
**파일**: `ai-tools.html`

#### Alpine.js AI 도구 대시보드 구조
```html
<main class="ai-tools-dashboard" x-data="aiToolsDashboard()" x-init="initDashboard()">
  <!-- 대시보드 헤더 -->
  <header class="dashboard-header">
    <h1>AI 생성 도구</h1>
    
    <!-- 사용량 통계 -->
    <div class="usage-stats">
      <div class="stat-item">
        <span class="label">이번 달 사용량</span>
        <span class="value" x-text="usageStats.monthlyUsage + '회'"></span>
        <div class="progress-bar">
          <div class="progress-fill" :style="`width: ${usageStats.usagePercentage}%`"></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-item">
        <span class="label">남은 크레딧</span>
        <span class="value" x-text="usageStats.remainingCredits + '개'"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-item">
        <span class="label">평균 품질</span>
        <span class="value" x-text="usageStats.averageQuality + '점'"></span>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 빠른 액션 -->
    <div class="quick-actions">
      <button class="btn-primary" @click="startQuickGeneration()" :disabled="!canGenerateContent">
        <svg class="icon" fill="none" stroke="currentColor">
          <path d="M13 10V3L4 14h7v7l9-11h-7z"></path>
        </svg>
        빠른 생성
      </button>
      <button class="btn-secondary" @click="openSettings()">설정</button>
    </div>
  </header>

  <!-- 사용 가능한 AI 도구들 -->
  <section class="available-tools">
    <h2>사용 가능한 AI 도구</h2>
    <div class="tools-grid">
      <template x-for="tool in availableTools" :key="tool.id">
        <div class="tool-card" :class="{ 'disabled': !tool.enabled }">
          <div class="tool-icon" :class="tool.iconClass">
            <svg x-html="tool.iconSvg"></svg>
          </div>
          
          <div class="tool-info">
            <h3 x-text="tool.name"></h3>
            <p x-text="tool.description"></p>
            
            <div class="tool-stats">
              <span>사용: <strong x-text="tool.usageCount + '회'"></strong></span>
              <span x-show="tool.averageRating">평점: <strong x-text="tool.averageRating + '★'"></strong></span>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div class="tool-actions">
            <button class="btn-tool-use" @click="useTool(tool.id)" 
                    :disabled="!tool.enabled || isProcessing[tool.id]"
                    :aria-label="tool.name + ' 사용하기'">
              <span x-show="!isProcessing[tool.id]">사용하기</span>
              <span x-show="isProcessing[tool.id]">processing...</span>
            </button>
            
            <button class="btn-tool-info" @click="showToolInfo(tool.id)">정보</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </template>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- 최근 생성 이력 -->
  <section class="recent-generations">
    <div class="section-header">
      <h2>최근 생성 이력</h2>
      <div class="header-actions">
        <button @click="toggleFilter()" :class="{ 'active': showFilters }">필터</button>
        <button @click="refreshHistory()" :disabled="isLoadingHistory">새로고침</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 필터 패널 -->
    <div x-show="showFilters" x-collapse class="filter-panel">
      <select x-model="filters.type" @change="applyFilters()">
        <option value="">모든 유형</option>
        <option value="education_plan">교육계획</option>
        <option value="content">학습 콘텐츠</option>
        <option value="assessment">평가 자료</option>
      </select>
      
      <select x-model="filters.status" @change="applyFilters()">
        <option value="">모든 상태</option>
        <option value="completed">완료</option>
        <option value="pending">검토 중</option>
        <option value="approved">승인됨</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 생성 이력 목록 -->
    <div class="generation-history">
      <template x-for="item in filteredGenerations" :key="item.id">
        <div class="generation-item">
          <div class="item-header">
            <span class="type-badge" :class="getTypeBadgeClass(item.type)" x-text="getTypeText(item.type)"></span>
            <h4 x-text="item.title"></h4>
            <time x-text="formatDate(item.created_at)"></time>
          </div>
          
          <div class="item-content">
            <div class="generation-meta">
              <span x-show="item.student_name">학생: <strong x-text="item.student_name"></strong></span>
              <span>생성시간: <span x-text="item.generation_time + 'ms'"></span></span>
            </div>
            
            <div class="quality-score" x-show="item.quality_score">
              <span>품질: </span>
              <div class="score-bar">
                <div class="score-fill" :style="`width: ${item.quality_score}%`"></div>
              </div>
              <span x-text="item.quality_score + '점'"></span>
            </div>
            
            <span class="status-badge" :class="getStatusBadgeClass(item.review_status)" 
                  x-text="getStatusText(item.review_status)"></span>
          </div>
          
          <div class="item-actions">
            <button @click="viewGeneration(item.id)">보기</button>
            <button x-show="canEdit(item)" @click="editGeneration(item.id)">수정</button>
            <button @click="duplicateGeneration(item.id)">복사</button>
            <button x-show="canDelete(item)" @click="deleteGeneration(item.id)" class="danger">삭제</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </template>
      
      <!-- 빈 상태 -->
      <div x-show="filteredGenerations.length === 0 && !isLoadingHistory" class="empty-state">
        <h3>생성 이력이 없습니다</h3>
        <p>AI 도구를 사용하여 첫 번째 콘텐츠를 생성해보세요.</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>
</main>

<script>
function aiToolsDashboard() {
  return {
    // 상태 데이터
    usageStats: { monthlyUsage: 0, remainingCredits: 0, averageQuality: 0, usagePercentage: 0 },
    availableTools: [],
    generationHistory: [],
    filteredGenerations: [],
    
    // UI 상태
    isLoading: false,
    isLoadingHistory: false,
    isProcessing: {},
    showFilters: false,
    filters: { type: '', status: '', period: 'month' },
    
    get canGenerateContent() {
      return this.usageStats.remainingCredits > 0 && !this.isLoading;
    },
    
    // 초기화
    async initDashboard() {
      await Promise.all([
        this.loadUsageStats(),
        this.loadAvailableTools(),
        this.loadGenerationHistory()
      ]);
    },
    
    async loadUsageStats() {
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/usage-stats');
      if (response.ok) this.usageStats = await response.json();
    },
    
    async loadAvailableTools() {
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/available');
      if (response.ok) this.availableTools = await response.json();
    },
    
    async loadGenerationHistory() {
      this.isLoadingHistory = true;
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/generation-history');
      if (response.ok) {
        const result = await response.json();
        this.generationHistory = result.data || [];
        this.applyFilters();
      }
      this.isLoadingHistory = false;
    },
    
    applyFilters() {
      let filtered = [...this.generationHistory];
      if (this.filters.type) filtered = filtered.filter(item => item.type === this.filters.type);
      if (this.filters.status) filtered = filtered.filter(item => item.review_status === this.filters.status);
      this.filteredGenerations = filtered;
    },
    
    // 도구 사용
    async useTool(toolId) {
      const tool = this.availableTools.find(t => t.id === toolId);
      if (!tool?.enabled) return;
      
      this.$set(this.isProcessing, toolId, true);
      
      const routes = {
        'education_plan': '/ai-tools/education-plan-generation.html',
        'content_generation': '/ai-tools/content-generation.html'
      };
      
      window.location.href = routes[tool.key] || `/ai-tools/${tool.key}.html`;
    },
    
    startQuickGeneration() { window.location.href = '/ai-tools/quick-generation.html'; },
    openSettings() { window.location.href = '/ai-tools/settings.html'; },
    toggleFilter() { this.showFilters = !this.showFilters; },
    refreshHistory() { this.loadGenerationHistory(); },
    
    // 유틸리티
    getTypeBadgeClass(type) {
      return { 'education_plan': 'badge-blue', 'content': 'badge-green', 'assessment': 'badge-yellow' }[type] || 'badge-gray';
    },
    getTypeText(type) {
      return { 'education_plan': '교육계획', 'content': '학습콘텐츠', 'assessment': '평가자료' }[type] || type;
    },
    getStatusBadgeClass(status) {
      return { 'completed': 'status-success', 'pending': 'status-warning', 'approved': 'status-success' }[status] || 'status-gray';
    },
    getStatusText(status) {
      return { 'completed': '완료', 'pending': '검토중', 'approved': '승인됨', 'rejected': '반려됨' }[status] || status;
    },
    formatDate(dateString) { return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString('ko-KR'); },
    canEdit(item) { return item.review_status !== 'approved'; },
    canDelete(item) { return ['draft', 'rejected'].includes(item.review_status); }
  };
}
</script>
```

#### 주요 특징
- **실시간 통계**: 사용량, 크레딧, 품질 지표 실시간 표시
- **도구 그리드**: 사용 가능한 AI 도구들 카드 형태로 표시
- **생성 이력**: 필터링, 정렬, 검색 기능 지원
- **HTMX 통합**: 실시간 상태 업데이트
- **Supabase Edge Functions**: AI 도구 백엔드 호출
- **UTF-8 안전성**: 한글 데이터 안전 처리
- **접근성**: ARIA 레이블, 키보드 네비게이션

### 5.2 교육 콘텐츠 AI 생성
**경로**: `/ai-tools/content-generation.html`
**파일**: `ai-tools/content-generation.html`

#### 주요 기능
- 개별화 학습 자료 생성
- 평가 문항 자동 생성
- 교수-학습 가이드 작성
- 다양한 난이도 변환
- 접근성 친화적 포맷 변환

#### Alpine.js 데이터 구조
```javascript
// 교육 콘텐츠 생성 상태 관리
const contentGenerationData = {
  // 학생 정보 및 컨텍스트
  selectedStudent: null,
  studentContext: {
    id: '',
    name: '',
    grade: '',
    disabilities: [],
    learningStyle: '',
    currentLevel: {}
  },
  
  // 생성 설정
  generationSettings: {
    contentType: 'worksheet', // worksheet, assessment, guide, activity
    subject: '',
    topic: '',
    difficulty: 'medium', // easy, medium, hard
    format: 'text', // text, visual, audio, mixed
    accessibility: {
      fontSize: 'medium',
      contrast: 'high',
      languageLevel: 'simple'
    }
  },
  
  // 프롬프트 빌더
  promptBuilder: {
    basePrompt: '',
    customInstructions: '',
    learningObjectives: [],
    evaluationCriteria: []
  },
  
  // 템플릿 관리
  templates: {
    categories: [],
    selectedTemplate: null,
    customTemplate: '',
    previewContent: ''
  },
  
  // 생성 결과
  generationResult: {
    isGenerating: false,
    progress: 0,
    content: '',
    qualityScore: 0,
    suggestions: [],
    errors: []
  },
  
  // UI 상태
  ui: {
    activeTab: 'setup', // setup, template, generate, review
    showAdvanced: false,
    showPreview: false
  }
};
```
